1-1: Every man is a human.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   SubClassOf(
      :man
      :human
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

<Ontology
    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <SubClassOf>
    <Class
	IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#man"/>
    <Class
	IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#human"/>
  </SubClassOf>
</Ontology>

2: Every human is a male or is a female.

         :male
         :female
      )
   )
)

    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"

	  IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#female"/>

</Ontology>

5: Everything that a goat eats is some grass.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   SubClassOf(
      ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
         ObjectInverseOf(
            :eat
         )
         :goat
      )
      :grass
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <SubClassOf>
    <ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
      <ObjectInverseOf>
	<ObjectProperty
	    IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#eat"/>
      </ObjectInverseOf>
      <Class
	  IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#goat"/>
    </ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
    <Class
	IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#grass"/>
  </SubClassOf>
</Ontology>

12: There is a woman who everybody likes.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   SubClassOf(
      owl:Thing
      ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
         :like
         ObjectOneOf(
            _:17775295470569263
         )
      )
   )
   ClassAssertion(
      :woman
      _:17775295470569263
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <SubClassOf>
    <Class IRI="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#Thing"/>
    <ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
      <ObjectProperty
	  IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#like"/>
      <ObjectOneOf>
	<NamedIndividual
	    IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#Ind17775295470569263"/>
      </ObjectOneOf>
    </ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
  </SubClassOf>
  <ClassAssertion>
    <Class
	IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#woman"/>
    <NamedIndividual
	IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#Ind17775295470569263"/>
  </ClassAssertion>
</Ontology>

13: Every man likes at least 3 things.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   SubClassOf(
      :man
      ObjectMinCardinality(
         3
         :like
         owl:Thing
      )
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

<Ontology
    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <SubClassOf>
    <Class
	IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#man"/>
    <ObjectMinCardinality cardinality="3">
      <ObjectProperty
	  IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#like"/>
      <Class IRI="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#Thing"/>
    </ObjectMinCardinality>
  </SubClassOf>
</Ontology>

15-1: If a thing A is taller than a thing that is taller than a thing C then A is taller than C.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>

      :tall
   )
)

<Ontology
    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">

    <ObjectProperty

15-2: If a dog is taller than a cat that is taller than a mouse then the dog is taller than the mouse.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :tall
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
         )
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :tall
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x5>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :dog
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :cat
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :mouse
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x5>)
         )
      )
      Head(
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :tall
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x5>)
         )
      )
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

<Ontology
    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <DLSafeRule>
    <Body>
      <ObjectPropertyAtom>
	<ObjectProperty
	    IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#tall"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x2"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x3"/>
      </ObjectPropertyAtom>
      <ObjectPropertyAtom>
	<ObjectProperty
	    IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#tall"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x3"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x5"/>
      </ObjectPropertyAtom>
      <ClassAtom>
	<Class
	    IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#dog"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x2"/>
      </ClassAtom>
      <ClassAtom>
	<Class
	    IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#cat"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x3"/>
      </ClassAtom>
      <ClassAtom>
	<Class
	    IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#mouse"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x5"/>
      </ClassAtom>
    </Body>
    <Head>
      <ObjectPropertyAtom>
	<ObjectProperty
	    IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#tall"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x2"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x5"/>
      </ObjectPropertyAtom>
    </Head>
  </DLSafeRule>
</Ontology>

      :write

18: Everything that somebody writes is a book or is a paper.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   ObjectPropertyRange(
      :write
      ObjectUnionOf(
         :book
         :paper
      )
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

<Ontology
    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <ObjectPropertyRange>
    <ObjectProperty
	IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#write"/>
    <ObjectUnionOf>
      <Class
	  IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#book"/>
      <Class
	  IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#paper"/>
    </ObjectUnionOf>

   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         ClassAtom(
            :man
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :dog
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
         )
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :own
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
         )

            :cat
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x4>)

            :own
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x4>)

            :like
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x4>)
         )
      )

         ClassAtom(
            :human
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x7>)

            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x7>)
         )
      )
   )
)

      </ClassAtom>
      <SameIndividualAtom>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x1"/>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#x7"/>
      </SameIndividualAtom>
    </Head>
  </DLSafeRule>
</Ontology>

93: If John likes Mary then Mary likes Bill.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   SubClassOf(
      ObjectIntersectionOf(
         ObjectOneOf(
            :Mary
         )
         ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
            ObjectInverseOf(
               :like
            )
            ObjectOneOf(
               :John
            )
         )
      )
      ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
         :like
         ObjectOneOf(
            <http://www.example.org/words#Bill>
         )
      )
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

<Ontology
    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <SubClassOf>
    <ObjectIntersectionOf>
      <ObjectOneOf>
	<NamedIndividual
	    IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#Mary"/>
      </ObjectOneOf>
      <ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
	<ObjectInverseOf>
	  <ObjectProperty
	      IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#like"/>
	</ObjectInverseOf>
	<ObjectOneOf>
	  <NamedIndividual
	      IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#John"/>
	</ObjectOneOf>
      </ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
    </ObjectIntersectionOf>
    <ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
      <ObjectProperty
	  IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#like"/>
      <ObjectOneOf>
	<NamedIndividual IRI="http://www.example.org/words#Bill"/>
      </ObjectOneOf>
    </ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
  </SubClassOf>
</Ontology>

    </ObjectMinCardinality>

	IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#John"/>
  </ClassAssertion>
</Ontology>

      :love
      ObjectHasSelf(
         :love
      )
   )
)

107: If a man likes Mary and Mary hates a dog then the man owns a car.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   SubClassOf(
      ObjectIntersectionOf(
         :man
         ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
            :like
            ObjectIntersectionOf(
               ObjectOneOf(
                  :Mary
               )
               ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
                  :hate
                  :dog
               )
            )
         )
      )
      ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
         :own
         :car
      )
   )
)

108: If a man likes Mary and Mary does not hate a dog then the man owns a car.

Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   SubClassOf(
      ObjectIntersectionOf(
         :man
         ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
            :like
            ObjectIntersectionOf(
               ObjectOneOf(
                  :Mary
               )
               ObjectComplementOf(
                  ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
                     :hate
                     :dog
                  )
               )
            )
         )
      )
      ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
         :own
         :car
      )
   )
)

111: Everybody's age is 31.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :age
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
         )
      )
      Head(
         SameIndividualAtom(
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
            int(
               31
            )
         )
      )
   )
)

error('Not an individual nor a SWRL variable',context(v_or_ie_to_xml/3,int(31)))

113: If somebody's age is 31 then his address is "Poland".

Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   SubClassOf(
      DataHasValue(
         :age
         "31"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>
      )
      DataHasValue(
         :address
         "Poland"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string>
      )
   )
)

121: If there is a number X then X + 1 = John.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         ClassAtom(
            :number
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
         )
      )
      Head(
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:equal>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg1>)
            :John
         )
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:add>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            "1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>
         )
      )
   )
)

error('Not a variable nor a literal',context(v_or_l_to_xml/3,'':'John'))
122: If 1.1 * 2 = 2.2 then 0.9 = 2 - 1.1.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:equal>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg2>)
            "2.2"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#double>
         )
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:multiply>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg2>)
            "1.1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#double>
            "2"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>
         )
      )
      Head(
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:equal>
            "0.9"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#double>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg3>)
         )
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:subtract>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg3>)
            "2"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>
            "1.1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#double>
         )
      )
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

<Ontology
    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <DLSafeRule>
    <Body>
      <BuiltInAtom IRI="http://www.w3.org/2003/11/swrlb#equal">
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#xg2"/>
	<Literal datatypeIRI="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#double">2.2</Literal>
      </BuiltInAtom>
      <BuiltInAtom IRI="http://www.w3.org/2003/11/swrlb#multiply">
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#xg2"/>
	<Literal datatypeIRI="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#double">1.1</Literal>
	<Literal datatypeIRI="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer">2</Literal>
      </BuiltInAtom>
    </Body>
    <Head>
      <BuiltInAtom IRI="http://www.w3.org/2003/11/swrlb#equal">
	<Literal datatypeIRI="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#double">0.9</Literal>
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#xg3"/>
      </BuiltInAtom>
      <BuiltInAtom IRI="http://www.w3.org/2003/11/swrlb#subtract">
	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#xg3"/>
	<Literal datatypeIRI="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer">2</Literal>
	<Literal datatypeIRI="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#double">1.1</Literal>
      </BuiltInAtom>
    </Head>
  </DLSafeRule>
</Ontology>

123: If E approaches 2 then 3.14 approaches Pi.
message(warning,word,1-8,Pi,Undefined word. Interpreted as a singular proper name.)

      Body(
         DataPropertyAtom(
            :approach
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            "2"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>
         )
      )
      Head(
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :approach
            real(
               3.14
            )
            :Pi
         )
      )
   )
)

         )

                  :ride
                  :car
               )

            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
         )

               ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
                  :ride
                  :bus

               ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
                  :ride
                  :bike
               )
            )
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
         )
      )

            :dog
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x8>)
         )

            :like
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x8>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
         )

            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x8>)
         )
      )
   )

message(warning,word,1-5,Estonia,Undefined word. Interpreted as a singular proper name.)

152: What is a country that borders Estonia or that Switzerland borders?
message(warning,word,1-7,Estonia,Undefined word. Interpreted as a singular proper name.)
message(warning,word,1-10,Switzerland,Undefined word. Interpreted as a singular proper name.)

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   SubClassOf(
      ObjectIntersectionOf(
         :country
         ObjectUnionOf(
            ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
               :border
               ObjectOneOf(
                  :Estonia
               )
            )
            ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
               ObjectInverseOf(
                  :border
               )
               ObjectOneOf(
                  :Switzerland
               )
            )
         )
      )
      owl:Thing
   )
)

185: If a man owns a car then the man likes the car and likes exactly 3 cats.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         ClassAtom(
            :man
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :car
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
         )
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :own
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
         )
      )
      Head(
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :like
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)

214: If there is a circle C and C's radius is R and C's area is S then S = Pi * (R * R) / 1.
message(warning,word,1-24,Pi,Undefined word. Interpreted as a singular proper name.)

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :area
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
         )
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :radius
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x5>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :circle
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
         )
      )
      Head(
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:equal>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg4>)
         )
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:divide>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg4>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg5>)
            "1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>
         )
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:multiply>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg5>)
            :Pi
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg6>)
         )
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:multiply>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg6>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x5>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x5>)
         )
      )
   )
)

error('Not a variable nor a literal',context(v_or_l_to_xml/3,'':'Pi'))

      Body(
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:equal>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg7>)
            "3"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>
         )
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:add>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg7>)
            "1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>
            "2"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>
         )
      )
      Head(
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:equal>
            "1"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#integer>

218: If a country X1 surrounds a territory X2 and the territory X2 is a part of a country X3 and it is false that the country X3 is the country X1 then the territory X2 is an enclave.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :part
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :country
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x4>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :territory
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
         )
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :surround
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x4>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :country
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
         )
         DifferentIndividualsAtom(
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x4>)
         )
      )
      Head(
         ClassAtom(
            :enclave
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x7>)
         )
         SameIndividualAtom(
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x7>)
         )
      )
   )
)

219: If "12" & "34" = "1234" then John owns at most 5 cars.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:equal>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg10>)
            "1234"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string>
         )
         BuiltInAtom(<swrlb:stringConcat>
            Variable(<urn:swrl#xg10>)
            "12"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string>
            "34"^^<http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string>
         )
      )
      Head(
         ClassAtom(
            ObjectMaxCardinality(
               5
               :own
               :car
            )
            :John
         )
      )
   )
)

	<Literal datatypeIRI="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string">1234</Literal>
      </BuiltInAtom>

	<Variable IRI="urn:swrl#xg10"/>
	<Literal datatypeIRI="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#string">12</Literal>

231: If John is rich then Mary is pretty.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         ClassAtom(
            :rich
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
         )
         SameIndividualAtom(
            :John
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
         )
      )
      Head(
         ClassAtom(
            :pretty
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
         )
         SameIndividualAtom(
            :Mary
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x3>)
         )
      )
   )
)

         :rich
         :famous
      )
   )

233: Every talented and beautiful woman is rich and famous and is smarter than her own husband.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   DLSafeRule(
      Body(
         ClassAtom(
            :woman
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :beautiful
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
         )
         SameIndividualAtom(
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x2>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :talented
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x4>)
         )
         SameIndividualAtom(
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x4>)
         )
      )
      Head(
         ClassAtom(
            :rich
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x6>)
         )
         ClassAtom(
            :famous
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x7>)
         )
         SameIndividualAtom(
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x6>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x7>)
         )
         SameIndividualAtom(
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x6>)
         )
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :smart
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x11>)
         )
         ObjectPropertyAtom(
            :husband
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x1>)
            Variable(<urn:swrl#x11>)
         )
      )
   )
)

         )
      )
   )

            _:814128422393801068
         )
         :fireman
      )
      :man
   )

      owl:Thing
      _:814128422393801068
   )
)

Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   ClassAssertion(
      ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
         :sister
         ObjectSomeValuesFrom(
            ObjectInverseOf(
               :like
            )
            ObjectOneOf(
               :John
            )
         )
      )
      :Mary
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

<Ontology
    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <ClassAssertion>
    <ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
      <ObjectProperty
	  IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#sister"/>
      <ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
	<ObjectInverseOf>
	  <ObjectProperty
	      IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#like"/>
	</ObjectInverseOf>
	<ObjectOneOf>
	  <NamedIndividual
	      IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#John"/>
	</ObjectOneOf>
      </ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
    </ObjectSomeValuesFrom>
    <NamedIndividual
	IRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#Mary"/>
  </ClassAssertion>
</Ontology>

            :alien
         )
      )
   )

281: John has at least 2 cats that at least 3 dogs like.

Prefix(:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test#>)
Prefix(ace:=<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ace#>)
Ontology(<http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test>
   ClassAssertion(
      ObjectMinCardinality(
         2
         :have
         ObjectIntersectionOf(
            :cat
            ObjectMinCardinality(
               3
               ObjectInverseOf(
                  :like
               )
               :dog
            )
         )
      )
      :John
   )
)

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>

<Ontology
    xml:base="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#"
    ontologyIRI="http://attempto.ifi.uzh.ch/ontologies/owlswrl/test">
  <ClassAssertion>
    <ObjectMinCardinality cardinality="2">
